mainpage The data structure section intro Introduction c oomph lib is big ! This \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_af8389ae6be77099ad63d360964d90450}{document}} gives \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} bottom up overview of the library \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_acdf437512dc428cd2c5e8b3aa8b92896}{s}} data structure \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} discusses how the various objects interact In addition to the detailed discussion provided the following doxygen generated lists indices provide quick access to the documentation of c oomph lib \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_acdf437512dc428cd2c5e8b3aa8b92896}{s}} we usually replace the list of arguments to \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a1fdf656642d185469f65e5cfd1eb41e2}{functions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e432636a4a6b59e504772b968782704}{by}} (...)\textquotesingle{} \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} explain the main input \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} output parameters in words. The full specifications of the interfaces may be found in the individual class documentation

\mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a5ee8c53ff4e7538382193801d5c0dcf4}{often}} abbreviated as dof b History b history \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a0666fd57a269ed17fd3cc7a808bd31ec}{values}} are but b not b the \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a0666fd57a269ed17fd3cc7a808bd31ec}{values}} at previous timesteps b Pinned c c c Mesh \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} c Problem subsection data Data The \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_ad22e1eba19a65ec7cdd50d59b6128aa8}{most}} elementary data structure in c oomph lib is c \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03b0383574e47211614b1d35905cb4c8}{Data}} (ha!). Consider the solution of \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} scalar P\+DE(e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} Poisson equation) with certain boundary conditions. The numerical solution of this \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a17412bdebdfe9ca84e9d46790fc5c041}{problem}} requires the computation of the function \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a0666fd57a269ed17fd3cc7a808bd31ec}{values}}(double precision numbers) at \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} finite number of spatial positions(the \textbackslash{}c \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a840078f64c4e152ec7f977fc08cf9155}{Nodes}}). \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a8f833a7a369b3afa91a144f664c6aaa4}{Typically}}

Time\+Stepper\mbox{[}Note\+:\+By default, we allocate the same amount of storage \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_a30c958e3d66b6db6e39e74dd5eb23db1}{for}} the history of the nodal positions as we do \mbox{\hyperlink{cfortran_8h_a30c958e3d66b6db6e39e74dd5eb23db1}{for}} the history of the nodal \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a0666fd57a269ed17fd3cc7a808bd31ec}{values}};e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_aa761080bc57113d682fcb4b66e35d084}{scheme}} is used to evaluate the time-\/derivatives of the \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_af2374cc183d898a3d5499aba088b219e}{that}} the same timestepping \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_aa761080bc57113d682fcb4b66e35d084}{scheme}} is used(\mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} the same amount of storage required) to determine the mesh \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a1d53daa8e93a1fa428e4506a4bedf87e}{velocities}} from the nodal positions.\mbox{]} For finite \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_acca8432f581d1782ef9e6f7ebe51cdb2}{elements}} in which the global \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_aecdcb19250d339765d0095e975875b2a}{position}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} point in an \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a23b5a245f0462b0a4823b0eb07a65baf}{element}} is determined \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e432636a4a6b59e504772b968782704}{by}} \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a0dbf3ebf11b527f1f8f1b9f494ba38e9}{interpolation}} from the {\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_ac9ebb4343c73c74aa1b4f977fadc3344}{endcode}} The default implementation of c the simplest possible implementation of \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03668dd8951154b5a0d25cfd2a9483d9}{a}} new \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a23b5a245f0462b0a4823b0eb07a65baf}{element}} requires only the specification of c we need to know which c \mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a03b0383574e47211614b1d35905cb4c8}{Data}} affects the residuals (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{the__data__structure_8txt_a9e4c2f9cf218e996a79932ca1af8a170}{and}} hence the Jacobian}]{matrix }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}
